Dedicated team allocation ensures 3-7 month completion.\',\n                etaMultiplier: 0.18\n            },\n            {\n                id: \'rush-level3\',\n                icon: \'🔥\',\n                title: \'Rush Level 3 — 2 to 3 Months\',\n                price: \'+35% of project total\',\n                nextStage: \'complete\',\n                details: \'High-priority fast-track delivery. Extended hours, dedicated resources, weekly milestone reviews.\',\n                etaMultiplier: 0.35\n            },\n            {\n                id: \'premiere-enterprise\',\n                icon: \'👑\',\n                title: \'Premiere Enterprise — 1-Week Demo\',\n                price: \'+65% upfront + $25/user/mo\',\n                nextStage: \'complete\',\n                details: \'Demo version delivered within 1 week. Your company runs on the beta platform immediately while the full build continues. $25/user/month billing applies until build completion.\',\n                etaMultiplier: 0.65,\n                perUserMonthly: 25\n            }\n        ]\n    }\n];\n\n/* --- CLOUD STAGE RENDERING ----------------------------------------------- */\nfunction showCloudStage(stageIndex) {\n    const stage = cloudTree[stageIndex];\n    if (!stage) return;\n\n    state.currentStageIndex = stageIndex;\n\n    const cloudStageEl = document.getElementById(\'cloud-stage\');\n    const backBtn = document.getElementById(\'back-btn\');\n    const nextPreview = document.getElementById(\'next-preview\');\n    const progressFill = document.getElementById(\'progress-fill\');\n\n    // Back button\n    if (backBtn) backBtn.style.display = state.cloudHistory.length > 0 ? \'block\' : \'none\';\n\n    // Progress bar\n    if (progressFill) {\n        const progress = Math.min(100, (stageIndex / (cloudTree.length - 1)) * 100);\n        progressFill.style.width = progress + \'%\';\n    }\n\n    // Next stage preview\n    if (nextPreview && stage.options[0]) {\n        const ns = stage.options[0].nextStage;\n        if (ns === \'complete\') {\n            nextPreview.textContent = \'Final step — review and generate your agreement\';\n        } else {\n            const found = cloudTree.find(s => s.id === ns);\n            nextPreview.textContent = found ? \'Up next: \' + found.title : \'\';\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Update topbar username\n    const configUser = document.getElementById(\'config-username\');\n    if (configUser && state.userName) configUser.textContent = state.userName + "\'s Configuration";\n\n    // Update topbar seal\n    const topbarSeal = document.getElementById(\'topbar-seal\');\n    if (topbarSeal && state.waxSealImage) topbarSeal.src = state.waxSealImage;\n\n    // Render stage\n    cloudStageEl.innerHTML = `\n        <div class="cloud-stage-inner">\n            <div class="stage-header">\n                <div class="stage-icon">${stage.icon || \'\'}</div>\n                <h2>${stage.title}</h2>\n                <p class="stage-desc">${stage.description}</p>\n            </div>\n            <div class="cloud-options-grid">\n                ${stage.options.map(opt => `\n                    <div class="cloud-option" data-option-id="${opt.id}" data-stage-id="${stage.id}">\n                        <div class="cloud-opt-icon">${opt.icon || \'◆\'}</div>\n                        <h3>${opt.title}</h3>\n                        <p class="cloud-opt-desc">${opt.details}</p>\n                        <div class="cloud-opt-price">${opt.price}</div>\n                    </div>\n                `).join(\'\')}\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    `;\n\n    // Attach click handlers\n    cloudStageEl.querySelectorAll(\'.cloud-option\').forEach(el => {\n        el.addEventListener(\'click\', () => handleCloudOption(stage.id, el.dataset.optionId));\n    });\n}\n\nfunction handleCloudOption(stageId, optionId) {\n    const stage = cloudTree.find(s => s.id === stageId);\n    if (!stage) return;\n    const selectedOption = stage.options.find(o => o.id === optionId);\n    if (!selectedOption) return;\n\n    // Store selection\n    state.preferences[stageId] = { ...selectedOption };\n\n    // History\n    state.cloudHistory.push({ stageId: stageId, stageIndex: state.currentStageIndex, optionId });\n\n    // Persist\n    fetch(\'/api/preferences\', {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ preferences: state.preferences })\n    }).catch(() => {});\n\n    // Navigate\n    if (selectedOption.nextStage === \'complete\') {\n        buildAndShowAgreement();\n    } else {\n        const nextIndex = cloudTree.findIndex(s => s.id === selectedOption.nextStage);\n        if (nextIndex >= 0) showCloudStage(nextIndex);\n    }\n}\n\n// Back navigation\ndocument.getElementById(\'back-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n    if (state.cloudHistory.length > 0) {\n        const last = state.cloudHistory.pop();\n        delete state.preferences[last.stageId];\n        fetch(\'/api/preferences\', {\n            method: \'POST\',\n            headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n            body: JSON.stringify({ preferences: state.preferences })\n        }).catch(() => {});\n        showCloudStage(last.stageIndex);\n    }\n});\n\n/* --- LANDING PAGE --------------------------------------------------------- */\nfunction handleNameEntry() {\n    const input = document.getElementById(\'name-input\');\n    const name = input ? input.value.trim() : \'\';\n    if (!name) { alert(\'Please enter your full name\'); return; }\n    state.userName = name;\n\n    fetch(\'/api/check-user\', {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ name })\n    })\n    .then(r => r.json())\n    .then(data => {\n        if (data.exists) {\n            const seal = document.getElementById(\'login-wax-seal\');\n            if (seal) seal.src = data.waxSeal || \'\';\n            showPage(\'login-page\');\n            initLoginSigPad();\n        } else {\n            showPage(\'password-page\');\n            startSealGeneration();\n        }\n    })\n    .catch(() => {\n        showPage(\'password-page\');\n        startSealGeneration();\n    });\n}\n\ndocument.getElementById(\'name-input\').addEventListener(\'keypress\', e => {\n    if (e.key === \'Enter\') handleNameEntry();\n});\ndocument.getElementById(\'enter-name-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', handleNameEntry);\n\n/* --- REGISTRATION --------------------------------------------------------- */\nfunction startSealGeneration() {\n    const generating = document.getElementById(\'seal-generating\');\n    const form = document.getElementById(\'signature-password-form\');\n    const result = document.getElementById(\'wax-seal-result\');\n    if (generating) generating.style.display = \'flex\';\n    if (form) form.style.display = \'none\';\n    if (result) result.style.display = \'none\';\n\n    setTimeout(() => {\n        if (generating) generating.style.display = \'none\';\n        if (form) form.style.display = \'block\';\n        initRegisterSigPad();\n    }, 3000);\n}\n\n/* --- SIGNATURE PAD FACTORY ----------------------------------------------- */\nfunction createSigPad(canvas) {\n    const ctx = canvas.getContext(\'2d\');\n    ctx.strokeStyle = \'#1a1a2e\';\n    ctx.lineWidth = 2.2;\n    ctx.lineCap = \'round\';\n    ctx.lineJoin = \'round\';\n\n    let drawing = false;\n    let pts = [];\n    let lastX = 0, lastY = 0;\n\n    function coords(e) {\n        const r = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();\n        const src = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;\n        return [src.clientX - r.left, src.clientY - r.top];\n    }\n    function down(e) {\n        e.preventDefault();\n        drawing = true;\n        [lastX, lastY] = coords(e);\n        pts.push({ x: lastX, y: lastY, t: Date.now() });\n    }\n    function move(e) {\n        if (!drawing) return;\n        e.preventDefault();\n        const [x, y] = coords(e);\n        ctx.beginPath();\n        ctx.moveTo(lastX, lastY);\n        ctx.lineTo(x, y);\n        ctx.stroke();\n        [lastX, lastY] = [x, y];\n        pts.push({ x, y, t: Date.now() });\n    }\n    function up() { drawing = false; }\n\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'mousedown\', down);\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'mousemove\', move);\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'mouseup\', up);\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'mouseout\', up);\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'touchstart\', down, { passive: false });\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'touchmove\', move, { passive: false });\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'touchend\', up);\n\n    return {\n        clear() { ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height); pts = []; },\n        getData() { return pts.length > 8 ? pts : null; },\n        getImage() { return canvas.toDataURL(\'image/png\'); }\n    };\n}\n\nfunction initRegisterSigPad() {\n    const canvas = document.getElementById(\'register-signature-pad\');\n    if (!canvas) return;\n    state.registerSigPad = createSigPad(canvas);\n    document.getElementById(\'clear-register-signature\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n        if (state.registerSigPad) state.registerSigPad.clear();\n    });\n}\n\nfunction initLoginSigPad() {\n    const canvas = document.getElementById(\'login-signature-pad\');\n    if (!canvas) return;\n    state.loginSigPad = createSigPad(canvas);\n    document.getElementById(\'clear-login-signature\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n        if (state.loginSigPad) state.loginSigPad.clear();\n    });\n}\n\n/* --- CREATE ACCOUNT ------------------------------------------------------- */\ndocument.getElementById(\'create-account-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n    const pw = document.getElementById(\'password\').value;\n    const pw2 = document.getElementById(\'confirm-password\').value;\n    const err = document.getElementById(\'password-error\');\n    err.textContent = \'\';\n\n    if (pw) {\n        if (pw.length < 6) { err.textContent = \'Password must be at least 6 characters\'; return; }\n        if (!/[!@#$%^&*(),.?":{}|<>]/.test(pw)) { err.textContent = \'Password must include a special character\'; return; }\n        if (!/\\d/.test(pw)) { err.textContent = \'Password must include a number\'; return; }\n        if (pw !== pw2) { err.textContent = \'Passwords do not match\'; return; }\n    }\n\n    const sigData = state.registerSigPad ? state.registerSigPad.getData() : null;\n    if (!sigData) { err.textContent = \'Please sign to create your signature passkey\'; return; }\n\n    fetch(\'/api/register\', {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ name: state.userName, password: pw || null, confirmPassword: pw2 || null, signatureData: sigData })\n    })\n    .then(r => r.json())\n    .then(data => {\n        if (data.success) {\n            state.userToken = data.token;\n            state.waxSealImage = data.waxSeal;\n            document.getElementById(\'signature-password-form\').style.display = \'none\';\n            document.getElementById(\'wax-seal-result\').style.display = \'block\';\n            document.getElementById(\'user-wax-seal\').src = data.waxSeal;\n            document.getElementById(\'unique-token\').textContent = data.token;\n        } else {\n            err.textContent = data.error || \'Registration failed\';\n        }\n    })\n    .catch(() => { err.textContent = \'Network error — please try again\'; });\n});\n\ndocument.getElementById(\'continue-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n    showPage(\'cloud-page\');\n    showCloudStage(0);\n});\n\n/* --- LOGIN ---------------------------------------------------------------- */\ndocument.getElementById(\'show-password-login\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n    const pwSection = document.getElementById(\'password-login-section\');\n    const visible = pwSection.style.display !== \'none\';\n    pwSection.style.display = visible ? \'none\' : \'block\';\n    state.usingPasswordBackup = !visible;\n});\n\ndocument.getElementById(\'login-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n    const nameEl = document.getElementById(\'login-name\');\n    const name = nameEl ? nameEl.value.trim() : state.userName;\n    const err = document.getElementById(\'login-error\');\n    const btn = document.getElementById(\'login-btn\');\n    err.textContent = \'\';\n\n    let sigData = null;\n    if (!state.usingPasswordBackup) {\n        sigData = state.loginSigPad ? state.loginSigPad.getData() : null;\n        if (!sigData) { err.textContent = \'Please sign to authenticate\'; return; }\n    }\n\n    const pw = state.usingPasswordBackup ? document.getElementById(\'login-password\').value : null;\n    if (!name) { err.textContent = \'Please enter your name\'; return; }\n\n    btn.textContent = \'Authenticating...\';\n    btn.disabled = true;\n\n    fetch(\'/api/login\', {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ name, password: pw, signatureData: sigData })\n    })\n    .then(r => r.json())\n    .then(data => {\n        btn.textContent = \'Authenticate\';\n        btn.disabled = false;\n        if (data.success) {\n            state.userName = name;\n            state.userToken = data.token;\n            state.waxSealImage = data.waxSeal;\n            loadPreferencesAndShowCloud();\n        } else {\n            err.textContent = data.error || \'Authentication failed\';\n            if (data.confidence !== undefined) {\n                err.textContent += ` (match: ${Math.round(data.confidence * 100)}%)`;\n            }\n        }\n    })\n    .catch(() => {\n        btn.textContent = \'Authenticate\';\n        btn.disabled = false;\n        err.textContent = \'Network error. Please try again.\';\n    });\n});\n\nfunction loadPreferencesAndShowCloud() {\n    fetch(\'/api/preferences\')\n        .then(r => r.json())\n        .then(data => {\n            state.preferences = data.preferences || {};\n            showPage(\'cloud-page\');\n            showCloudStage(0);\n        })\n        .catch(() => {\n            showPage(\'cloud-page\');\n            showCloudStage(0);\n        });\n}\n\n/* --- AGREEMENT BUILDER ---------------------------------------------------- */\nfunction computeTotalLabel() {\n    let base = 0;\n    let monthly = 0;\n\n    // Base project cost\n    const pt = state.preferences[\'project-type\'];\n    if (pt && pt.basePrice) base += pt.basePrice;\n    const wt = state.preferences[\'website-type\'];\n    if (wt && wt.basePrice) base += wt.basePrice;\n    const st = state.preferences[\'server-type\'];\n    if (st && st.basePrice) base += st.basePrice;\n    const stt = state.preferences[\'startup-type\'];\n    if (stt && stt.basePrice) base += stt.basePrice;\n\n    // Addon one-time costs\n    const wf = state.preferences[\'website-features\'];\n    if (wf && wf.addonPrice) base += wf.addonPrice;\n    const sa = state.preferences[\'server-addons\'];\n    if (sa && sa.addonPrice) monthly += sa.addonPrice;\n    const sta = state.preferences[\'startup-addons\'];\n    if (sta && sta.addonPrice) base += sta.addonPrice;\n\n    // Hosting\n    const hosting = state.preferences[\'hosting\'];\n    if (hosting && hosting.monthlyAddon) monthly += hosting.monthlyAddon;\n\n    // Ownership\n    const own = state.preferences[\'ownership\'];\n    if (own && own.monthly) monthly += own.monthly;\n\n    // AI\n    const ai = state.preferences[\'ai\'];\n    if (ai && ai.aiAddon) monthly += ai.aiAddon;\n\n    // Maintenance\n    const maint = state.preferences[\'maintenance\'];\n    if (maint && maint.maintenanceAddon) monthly += maint.maintenanceAddon;\n\n    // Addons\n    const addons = state.preferences[\'addons\'];\n    if (addons) {\n        if (addons.addonOneTime) base += addons.addonOneTime;\n        if (addons.addonMonthly) monthly += addons.addonMonthly;\n    }\n\n    // ETA Rush surcharge\n    const eta = state.preferences[\'eta-rush\'];\n    if (eta && eta.etaMultiplier && eta.etaMultiplier > 0) {\n        const surcharge = Math.round(base * eta.etaMultiplier);\n        base += surcharge;\n    }\n    if (eta && eta.perUserMonthly) {\n        monthly += eta.perUserMonthly; // per-user base estimate\n    }\n\n    let label = \'\';\n    if (base > 0) label += `Est. $${base.toLocaleString()} CAD one-time`;\n    if (monthly > 0) label += (label ? \' + \' : \'\') + `$${monthly.toLocaleString()}/mo`;\n    return label || \'Custom pricing — contact for quote\';\n}\n\nfunction buildAndShowAgreement() {\n    const prefs = state.preferences;\n    const totalLabel = computeTotalLabel();\n\n    // Build summary rows\n    const rows = Object.keys(prefs).map(key => {\n        const p = prefs[key];\n        return `\n            <tr>\n                <td>${p.title || key}</td>\n                <td>${p.price || \'—\'}</td>\n                <td>${(p.details || \'\').substring(0, 80)}${p.details && p.details.length > 80 ? \'...\' : \'\'}</td>\n            </tr>\n        `;\n    }).join(\'\');\n\n    const agType = (() => {\n        const own = prefs[\'ownership\'];\n        if (own && own.optionId === \'subscription\') return \'Subscription Services Agreement\';\n        if (own && own.optionId === \'full-ownership\') return \'Full Stack Development Agreement\';\n        const pt = prefs[\'project-type\'];\n        if (pt && pt.id === \'startup-design\') return \'Brand & Identity Services Agreement\';\n        if (pt && pt.id === \'server-it\') return \'IT Services Agreement\';\n        if (pt && pt.id === \'simple-website\') return \'Website Development Agreement\';\n        return \'Custom Development Agreement\';\n    })();\n\n    state.agreementData.type = agType;\n    state.agreementData.totalLabel = totalLabel;\n\n    const content = `\n        <div class="agreement-summary-wrap">\n            <h2 class="summary-title">Configuration Summary</h2>\n            <p class="summary-client">Prepared for: <strong>${state.userName}</strong></p>\n            <table class="config-summary-table">\n                <thead>\n                    <tr><th>Selection</th><th>Price</th><th>Details</th></tr>\n                </thead>\n                <tbody>${rows}</tbody>\n            </table>\n            <div class="summary-total-block">\n                <span class="total-label">Estimated Investment:</span>\n                <span class="total-value">${totalLabel}</span>\n            </div>\n            <p class="summary-note">* All prices are in Canadian Dollars (CAD) and represent estimates based on your selections. \n               Final quote will be confirmed upon project scoping. Alberta HST applies where applicable.</p>\n        </div>\n    `;\n\n    document.getElementById(\'agreement-content\').innerHTML = content;\n    document.getElementById(\'agreement-title\').textContent = agType;\n    const sealImg = document.getElementById(\'agreement-wax-seal-img\');\n    if (sealImg && state.waxSealImage) sealImg.src = state.waxSealImage;\n\n    showPage(\'agreement-page\');\n    initScrollIndicator();\n}\n\n/* --- AGREEMENT PAGE ------------------------------------------------------- */\nfunction initScrollIndicator() {\n    const scrollArea = document.getElementById(\'agreement-scroll-area\');\n    const indicator = document.getElementById(\'scroll-indicator\');\n    if (!scrollArea || !indicator) return;\n\n    scrollArea.addEventListener(\'scroll\', () => {\n        const { scrollTop, scrollHeight, clientHeight } = scrollArea;\n        if (scrollTop + clientHeight >= scrollHeight - 20) {\n            indicator.style.opacity = \'0\';\n        }\n    });\n}\n\ndocument.getElementById(\'agree-checkbox\').addEventListener(\'change\', e => {\n    const sigSection = document.getElementById(\'signature-section\');\n    if (sigSection) sigSection.style.display = e.target.checked ? \'block\' : \'none\';\n    if (e.target.checked) {\n        const seal = document.getElementById(\'signature-wax-seal\');\n        if (seal && state.waxSealImage) seal.src = state.waxSealImage;\n        initAgreementSigPad();\n    }\n});\n\nfunction initAgreementSigPad() {\n    const canvas = document.getElementById(\'signature-pad\');\n    if (!canvas) return;\n    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth || 600;\n    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight || 200;\n    state.agreementSigPad = createSigPad(canvas);\n}\n\ndocument.getElementById(\'clear-signature-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n    if (state.agreementSigPad) state.agreementSigPad.clear();\n    else {\n        const c = document.getElementById(\'signature-pad\');\n        if (c) c.getContext(\'2d\').clearRect(0, 0, c.width, c.height);\n    }\n});\n\ndocument.getElementById(\'finalize-agreement-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', finalizeAgreement);\n\nfunction finalizeAgreement() {\n    const email = document.getElementById(\'client-email\').value.trim();\n    const phone = document.getElementById(\'client-phone\').value.trim();\n    const errEl = document.getElementById(\'finalize-error\');\n    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = \'\';\n\n    if (!email || !phone) {\n        if (errEl) errEl.textContent = \'Please provide both email and phone number\';\n        return;\n    }\n    if (!email.includes(\'@\')) {\n        if (errEl) errEl.textContent = \'Please enter a valid email address\';\n        return;\n    }\n\n    const canvas = document.getElementById(\'signature-pad\');\n    const signatureData = canvas ? canvas.toDataURL(\'image/png\') : \'\';\n\n    state.agreementData.clientEmail = email;\n    state.agreementData.clientPhone = phone;\n\n    const btn = document.getElementById(\'finalize-agreement-btn\');\n    if (btn) { btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = \'Sealing Agreement...\'; }\n\n    // Save signature\n    fetch(\'/api/signature\', {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ signatureData })\n    })\n    .then(r => r.json())\n    .then(sigData => {\n        if (!sigData.success) throw new Error(\'Failed to save signature\');\n        state.agreementData.clientSignature = sigData.signaturePath;\n\n        // Save agreement\n        return fetch(\'/api/agreement\', {\n            method: \'POST\',\n            headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n            body: JSON.stringify({\n                agreementType: state.agreementData.type,\n                preferences: state.preferences\n            })\n        });\n    })\n    .then(r => r.json())\n    .then(agrData => {\n        if (!agrData.success) throw new Error(\'Failed to save agreement\');\n\n        // Generate contract\n        return fetch(\'/api/generate-contract\', {\n            method: \'POST\',\n            headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n            body: JSON.stringify({\n                preferences: state.preferences,\n                clientSignature: state.agreementData.clientSignature,\n                clientEmail: state.agreementData.clientEmail,\n                clientPhone: state.agreementData.clientPhone,\n                totalLabel: state.agreementData.totalLabel,\n                agreementType: state.agreementData.type\n            })\n        });\n    })\n    .then(r => r.json())\n    .then(contractData => {\n        if (!contractData.success) throw new Error(contractData.error || \'Failed to generate contract\');\n\n        state.agreementData.contractId = contractData.agreementId;\n\n        // Save to localStorage for contract viewer\n        localStorage.setItem(\'contractData\', JSON.stringify({\n            userName: state.userName,\n            waxSealImage: state.waxSealImage,\n            preferences: state.preferences,\n            clientSignature: state.agreementData.clientSignature,\n            clientEmail: state.agreementData.clientEmail,\n            clientPhone: state.agreementData.clientPhone,\n            totalLabel: state.agreementData.totalLabel,\n            agreementType: state.agreementData.type\n        }));\n\n        showSuccessPage(contractData.agreementId);\n    })\n    .catch(err => {\n        if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = \'🔏 Seal & Finalize Agreement\'; }\n        if (errEl) errEl.textContent = \'Error: \' + err.message;\n        console.error(err);\n    });\n}\n\n/* --- SUCCESS PAGE --------------------------------------------------------- */\nfunction showSuccessPage(agreementId) {\n    const totalLabel = state.agreementData.totalLabel || computeTotalLabel();\n    const projectType = state.preferences[\'project-type\'] ? state.preferences[\'project-type\'].title : \'Custom Project\';\n    const etaOption = state.preferences[\'eta-rush\'];\n    const etaLabel = etaOption ? etaOption.title : \'Standard Timeline\';\n    const tokenId = agreementId || (\'MM-\' + Date.now().toString(36).toUpperCase());\n\n    // Generate Digital Token of Excellence\n    const tokenDisplay = `\n        <div class="token-of-excellence">\n            <div class="token-outer-glow"></div>\n            <div class="token-card">\n                <div class="token-header">\n                    <div class="token-mm-icon">\n                        <svg viewBox="0 0 100 60" width="80" height="48" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                            <text x="0" y="50" font-family="Cinzel Decorative, serif" font-size="58" font-weight="900"\n                                  fill="none" stroke="url(#tg)" stroke-width="1.5" letter-spacing="-8">MM</text>\n                            <defs>\n                                <linearGradient id="tg" x1="0" y1="0" x2="100%" y2="0">\n                                    <stop offset="0%" stop-color="#f5c842"/>\n                                    <stop offset="50%" stop-color="#fff"/>\n                                    <stop offset="100%" stop-color="#f5c842"/>\n                                </linearGradient>\n                            </defs>\n                        </svg>\n                    </div>\n                    <div class="token-brand-text">METHOD MEDIA</div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="token-divider"></div>\n                <div class="token-title">Digital Token of Excellence</div>\n                <div class="token-project-name">${projectType}</div>\n                <div class="token-meta-grid">\n                    <div class="token-meta-item">\n                        <span class="tmeta-label">Client</span>\n                        <span {'role': 'assistant', 'content': 'Yes—there are several high-impact improvements you can make, and there are also some real issues/risks in the current codebase based on what I see from the last changes.\n\n## Improvements (highest value first)\n\n### 1) Separate the “paths” cleanly (website vs software vs IT vs design)\nRight now the configurator is a single linear tree, but your product is really multiple funnels. You’ll get better UX (and fewer pricing/math bugs) if you model it like:\n\n- **Choose category** → enters a **category-specific flow**\n- Each flow has its own steps and completion rules\n- At the end, a unified “Review + Agreement + Invoice” step runs\n\nThis makes it much easier to:\n- Tailor copy and pricing per category\n- Avoid showing irrelevant steps (ex: AI/hosting for startup brand design)\n- Avoid bugs from “missing preferences” when a path doesn’t go through certain stages\n\nImplementation idea: treat each category as a `flowId` with its own `stages[]`, instead of one global `cloudTree`.\n\n---\n\n### 2) Pricing engine: make it data-driven and consistent\nYour current pricing is a mix of:\n- text price strings (for display)\n- `basePrice`, `addonPrice`, `monthly`, multipliers, etc.\n\nThat’s workable, but it becomes fragile quickly.\n\nBetter pattern:\n- each option has a structured pricing object, e.g.\n  ```js\n  pricing: { oneTime: 3400, monthly: 0, perUserMonthly: 0, percentOfOneTime: 0 }\n  ```\n- the UI renders those values into strings\n- the invoice uses the structured numbers (not parsing strings)\n\nThis lets you produce a reliable **itemized invoice** and makes “rush %” always correct.\n\n---\n\n### 3) Add a real “cart / review” step before contract signing\nBefore the agreement page, add a Review page that:\n- shows all selections\n- lets the client edit earlier steps\n- shows subtotal, rush surcharge, monthly items, per-user items, taxes (if you want)\n- shows required disclaimers (e.g., “estimates, final quote after discovery”)\n\nThis reduces confusion and client churn.\n\n---\n\n### 4) Make the “Première Enterprise” logic explicit and captured\nYour “Première Enterprise” option includes special terms:\n- demo within 1 week\n- client runs beta while you iterate\n- $25/user/month until completion if logins exist\n\nBest approach:\n- add an extra question when that option is selected:\n  - “Does this build include user logins?” (Yes/No)\n  - “Estimated number of users during beta” (number input)\n- then invoice can compute `users * 25/mo`\n\nRight now it just adds `$25` without knowing user count.\n\n---\n\n### 5) Brand experience: use your uploaded imagery as a theme system\nYou can get a much more “Method Media art experience” by turning your visuals into a reusable theme:\n\n- background gradients derived from the ring colors\n- consistent glow colors (gold/orange/purple/cyan)\n- “wax seal” as an unlock animation across steps\n- page transitions that feel like “forging” rather than switching\n\nTechnically: create a `theme.css` with variables:\n```css\n:root {\n  --mm-gold: #f5c842;\n  --mm-orange: #f5820a;\n  --mm-purple: #a855f7;\n  --mm-cyan: #00e5ff;\n}\n```\nand apply consistently.\n\n---\n\n## Errors / issues I see (important)\n\n### 1) **Your `app.js` “complete rewrite” likely broke backend compatibility**\nIn the rewritten `app.js`, I see API calls like:\n\n- `POST /api/check-user` sending `{ name }`\n- `POST /api/register` sending `{ name, password, confirmPassword, signatureData }`\n- `POST /api/login` sending `{ name, password, signatureData }`\n\nBut earlier in your server you used fields like:\n- `username` (not `name`)\n- signature image vs signature point arrays\n- different payload structure\n\nIf the server expects `{ username }` and the frontend sends `{ name }`, you’ll get silent failures or unexpected “user not found” behavior.\n\n**Fix:** align client/server contract strictly:\n- choose `username` everywhere (recommended)\n- update `app.js` to use the same field names your server routes expect\n\nThis is the #1 thing I would verify immediately.\n\n---\n\n### 2) **Duplicate / inconsistent signature pad implementations**\nYour app.js now contains a new `createSigPad(canvas)` function (canvas element passed) that conflicts conceptually with the older style you had (canvasId-based + returning `isEmpty()` etc).\n\nThat’s not automatically fatal, but it increases the odds that:\n- signatures are not recorded properly\n- “empty signature” checks are wrong\n- login signature comparison logic becomes inconsistent\n\n**Fix:** keep one signature pad module and use it for register/login/agreement.\n\n---\n\n### 3) **Stages and totals: calculation inconsistencies**\nIn `computeTotalLabel()` you add:\n\n- `website-features` into base\n- `server-addons` into monthly (but `server-addons` has mixed hourly/monthly strings)\n- “remote-support” is displayed as `$299-$599/month` but you store `addonPrice: 450` (which is neither 299 nor 599)\n\nSo your “monthly total” can be misleading vs what the user selected.\n\n**Fix:** use structured pricing objects and compute from those. If you keep ranges, store `minMonthly`, `maxMonthly`, etc.\n\n---\n\n### 4) **Flow bug: “hosting” stage appears even for branding/IT paths**\nYou added a “hosting-na” option, but the flow still routes startup design add-ons → `hosting`. That means branding clients see hosting, ownership, AI, maintenance, etc., which doesn’t fit.\n\nThis is a UX bug (and a business logic bug) unless you intended to upsell SaaS hosting on brand packages.\n\n**Fix:** separate flows per category or conditionally skip stages.\n\n---\n\n### 5) **Agreement generation uses `/api/agreement` in rewritten app.js**\nIn your server.js earlier, the main finalize flow used:\n- `/api/signature`\n- `/api/generate-contract`\n- plus other endpoints\n\nBut the rewritten app.js calls `/api/agreement` (which may not exist, depending on your server.js version).\n\nIf `/api/agreement` is missing, finalize will fail.\n\n**Fix:** verify server has `/api/agreement` route; {'role': 'assistant', 'content': 'Nothing *has* to change about your actual price points. What needs to change is **how pricing is represented and calculated in code**, so you can reliably:\n\n- compute totals (one‑time vs monthly vs rush %)\n- generate an itemized invoice\n- avoid contradictions (UI shows one thing, totals/invoice compute something else)\n\n### What would change (exactly)\n\n#### 1) From “price as display text” → “price as numbers + display text”\nRight now many options use:\n- `price: "$2,800 – $4,500 CAD"` (a string meant for humans)\n- plus sometimes `basePrice: 3500` or `addonPrice: 450` (a number used by code)\n\nThat becomes inconsistent quickly because the string and the number can drift apart.\n\n**Change:** keep your attractive displayed ranges exactly as you like, but also store the numeric range explicitly:\n\nExample (website business site):\n```js\n{\n  title: "Business Website (5–10 pages)",\n  priceLabel: "$2,800 – $4,500 CAD",     // what the customer sees (your marketing)\n  pricing: { oneTimeMin: 2800, oneTimeMax: 4500, monthlyMin: 0, monthlyMax: 0 },\n  nextStage: "website-features"\n}\n```\n\nSo: **your visible pricing doesn’t need to increase**—we just stop the app from “guessing” totals using random single values.\n\n---\n\n#### 2) Totals become “range aware” instead of picking a single made-up number\nCurrently the code often picks a single `basePrice` (like 3500) even though the UI says “$2,800–$4,500”.\n\nThat can produce invoices like:\n- UI: $2,800–$4,500  \n- Invoice total: based on $3,500 + rush multiplier  \nWhich might be OK, but it’s not transparent and can create disputes.\n\n**Change:** totals show ranges when ranges are selected:\n\n- **One-time total (estimate):** `$3,430 – $5,280 CAD`\n- **Monthly total (if any):** `$199 – $399 / month`\n\nThis actually supports your strategy (attractive pricing) because it lets you show **low entry ranges** clearly without your backend accidentally calculating higher.\n\n---\n\n#### 3) Rush fees become mathematically correct\nYour rush options are percentage-based (+18%, +35%, +65%).  \nIf the base is a range, the rush should apply to the range too.\n\nSo instead of:\n- Base = 3500 (hardcoded)\n- Rush = 18% of 3500\n\nIt becomes:\n- Base min/max = 2800/4500\n- Rush = 18% of min/max\n\nInvoice line becomes:\n- Rush surcharge (18%): `$504 – $810`\n\nAgain: not more expensive—just accurate.\n\n---\n\n#### 4) Monthly items stop being “fake numbers”\nRight now you have items like:\n- “Remote IT Support Plan: $299–$599/month” but code stores `addonPrice: 450` (one number)\n- “On-site support: $125/hour” stored as `addonPrice: 125` (but that’s not monthly)\n\n**Change:** for items that are hourly or variable, invoices should show them as:\n- “On-site support: $125/hour (as needed)” and **not** add it into monthly totals unless a quantity is chosen.\n\nSo the app needs pricing types:\n- fixed monthly\n- fixed one-time\n- range estimate\n- hourly (not totaled unless quantity provided)\n- per-user monthly (Première Enterprise)\n\nThis helps you stay “non-inflated” because it prevents inflated totals caused by wrong assumptions.\n\n---\n\n### What does NOT need to change\n- Your **marketing-friendly price ranges**\n- Your strategy of being competitively priced vs “hyper inflated tech companies”\n- The wording that emphasizes “high value / engineered / unique experience”\n\nIf anything, a better pricing engine helps you *sell that positioning* more credibly because:\n- invoices match the quote ranges\n- rush math is clean\n- clients see exactly what they selected\n\n---\n\n### My recommendation (so you keep your attractive pricing)\nKeep your displayed ranges exactly as-is, but implement a pricing object per option:\n\n**Minimum required fields per option:**\n- `priceLabel` (string for UI)\n- `pricing.oneTimeMin`, `pricing.oneTimeMax`\n- `pricing.monthlyMin`, `pricing.monthlyMax`\n- optional `pricing.percentOfOneTime` (rush)\n- optional `pricing.perUserMonthly` (Première Enterprise)\n\nThen totals/invoices are computed from numeric fields only.\n\n---\n\nIf you tell me: **Do you want invoices to show ranges, or do you want invoices to show a single number (like a “starting from” price)?**  \nThat choice affects the exact invoice format.'}
